<ol><li>Tolstoyan, Tolstoyist <i>(female)</i></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***толстый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>то́лстый</a> (626)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tъlstъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>то́лстый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tólstyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:толща.html>то́лще</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">толсте́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thick</li>
<li>large, big</li>
<li>stout, fat
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1866</b>,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">Фёдор достое́вский</span> (Fyodor Dostoyevsky),  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9F%D1%80%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D1%83%D0%BF%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%B5_%D0%B8_%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%BA%D0%B0%D0%B7%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%B5Russian" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Преступление и наказание"><a href = vnd.unilang:преступление.html>Преступле́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ние</a></a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Prestuplenije i nakazánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></cite>  | <p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толстяк.html>толстя́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tolstják</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толстяк.html>толстяка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толстяк.html>толстяки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толстяк.html>толстяко́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толстячок.html>толстя́чка</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толстуха.html>толсту́ха</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">толсту́шка</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толстячок.html>толстячо́к</a></b>)
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толчок.html>толчо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tolčók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толчок.html>толчка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толчок.html>толчки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толчок.html>толчко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>push, impulse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:толчок.html>толчо́к</a></b> чему́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">davátʹ/datʹ <b>tolčók</b> čemú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stimulate something off / to give impetus to something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> toilet (fixture), toilet bowl</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> flea market</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:толща.html>то́лща</a> (18536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tъlstъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толща.html>то́лща</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tólšča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толща.html>то́лщи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толща.html>то́лщи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толща.html>то́лщ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thickness</li>
<li>stratum, thick layer, depth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:толща.html>то́лща</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tólšča</b> vody</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the water column</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:толща.html>то́лща</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порода.html>поро́д</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tólšča</b> poród</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the rock strata</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:народный.html>наро́дные</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:толща.html>то́лщи</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">naródnyje <b>tólšči</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the mass of the people</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***только.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> (39)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*toliko</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tólʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>only, but
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak tólʹko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">as soon as</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lišʹ tólʹko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">no sooner ... than</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jedvá <b>tólʹko</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">no sooner ... than</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tólʹko</b> by</i> ― <span class="e-translation">if only</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:томатный.html>тома́тный</a> (19869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:томат.html>тома́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tomát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***томительный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:томительный.html>томи́тельный</a> (12919)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:томить.html>томи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tomítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:томительный.html>томи́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tomítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>agonizing, painful, oppressive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:томительный.html>томи́тельная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жар.html>жара</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tomítelʹnaja</b> žara</i> ― <span class="e-translation">oppressive heat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:томительный.html>томи́тельная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоска́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tomítelʹnaja</b> toská</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mortal anguish</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tiresome, tedious, trying
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:томительный.html>томи́тельная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скука.html>ску́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tomítelʹnaja</b> skúka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">deadly boredom</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>stirring, titillating, tantalizing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:томительный.html>томи́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:аромат.html>арома́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tomítelʹnyj</b> aromát</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stirring/titillating/tantalizing aroma</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***томить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:томить.html>томи́ть</a> (11627)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">томити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tomiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tomiti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*TēmH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:томить.html>томи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tomítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to weary <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with a rather negative intention</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to torment, to torture, to languish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stew</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:томиться.html>томи́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tomítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li>(no equivalent)</li>

***томиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:томиться.html>томи́ться</a> (8386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:томить.html>томи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tomítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:томиться.html>томи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tomítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to pine <i>(for)</i>, to languish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:томиться.html>томи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожидание.html>ожида́нием</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tomítʹsja</b> ožidánijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be in an agony of suspense</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:томиться.html>томи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жажда.html>жа́ждой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tomítʹsja</b> žáždoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be parched with thirst; pant/pine for a drink</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:томиться.html>томи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жажда.html>жа́ждой</a> чего́-либо (<a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ть</a> чего́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tomítʹsja</b> žáždoj čevó-libo (óčenʹ želátʹ čevó-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">thirst for smth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:томиться.html>томи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плена.html>плену́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьме́</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tomítʹsja</b> v plenú (v tjurʹmé)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">languish in captivity (prison)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:томиться.html>томи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоско́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tomítʹsja</b> toskój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pine away</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:томиться.html>томи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родина.html>ро́дине</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tomítʹsja</b> po ródine</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pine for one's homeland</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stew</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:томить.html>томи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tomítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***тон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>тон</a> (1491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tonus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τόνος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tónos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cf. French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">ton</i>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонус.html>то́нус</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tónus</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>тон</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ton</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>то́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>то́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>тоно́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>то́нов</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <br />
<strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>тон</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ton</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>то́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>тона́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>тоно́в</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tone, plural: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>то́ны</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tóny</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">тона́льный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tonálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тональность.html>тона́льность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tonálʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тональность.html>тона́льности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тональность.html>тона́льности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тональность.html>тона́льностей</a></b>)

***тонировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонировать.html>тони́ровать</a> (29901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>тон</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ton</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонировать.html>тони́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tonírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to reproduce the full sound of (a musical or spoken text)</li>
<li>to decorate, to tint, to tone <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to touch up, giving a desired color or tint</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to set the tone, to prescribe the manner of behavior</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">тони́рование</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tonírovanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">тониро́вка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">toniróvka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***тонкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонкий.html>то́нкий</a> (767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тънъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tŭnŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tьnъkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкий.html>то́нкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tónkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)то́ньше</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тончайший.html>тонча́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thin</li>
<li>slim, slender</li>
<li>small, fine, delicate</li>
<li>fine, high-quality <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of food, wine, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>subtle</li>
<li>keen</li>
<li>high <i>(voice)</i></li></ol>
